	<nav id="kadence-breadcrumbs" aria-label="Breadcrumbs"  class="kadence-breadcrumbs"><div class="kadence-breadcrumb-container"><span><a href="https://turnrowtable.com/" itemprop="url" class="kadence-bc-home" ><span>Home</span></a></span> <span class="bc-delimiter">/</span> <span><a href="https://turnrowtable.com/category/turnrow-table-recipes/" itemprop="url" ><span>Recipes</span></a></span> <span class="bc-delimiter">/</span> <span class="kadence-bread-current">Simple Skillet Apple Cobbler</span></div></nav>		<div class="entry-taxonomies">

				<a href="https://turnrowtable.com/category/turnrow-table-recipes/" rel="tag">Recipes</a>			</span>

		<h1 class="entry-title">Simple Skillet Apple Cobbler</h1></header><!-- .entry-header -->

<div class="entry-content single-content">
	<input class="jpibfi" type="hidden"><div class="wprm-recipe wprm-recipe-snippet wprm-recipe-template-olive-snippit-2"><a href="#recipe" data-recipe="18660" style="color: #333333;" class="wprm-recipe-jump wprm-recipe-link wprm-jump-to-recipe-shortcode wprm-block-text-normal"><span class="wprm-recipe-icon wprm-recipe-jump-icon"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16"><g class="nc-icon-wrapper" fill="#e0d0c7"><path d="M11.943,5.269A.5.5,0,0,0,11.5,5h-7a.5.5,0,0,0-.409.787l3.5,5a.5.5,0,0,0,.818,0l3.5-5A.5.5,0,0,0,11.943,5.269Z" fill="#e0d0c7"></path></g></svg></span> Jump to Recipe</a>






<div class="recipe-header-snippet">





</div></div>


<p class="has-text-align-center" style="font-size:12px"><em>This post may contain affiliate links, please see&nbsp;</em><a href="https://turnrowtable.com/privacy-policy-2/">privacy policy</a><em>&nbsp;for details.</em></p>



<p class="has-text-align-center"><em>Savor a southern apple cobbler with a biscuit topping—cinnamon-spiced apples and a buttery crust for a delightful treat.</em></p>



<p class="has-text-align-center">This skillet apple cobbler with biscuit topping. This is my favorite biscuit recipe on top of a brown sugar, cinnamon fried apple filling. This is so decadent and fluffy. You have to top with vanilla ice cream while it&#8217;s hot. You cannot beat this classic southern dessert.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img decoding="async" width="683" height="1024" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20683%201024'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Ok. </div>


<p class="has-text-align-center">I love this apple cobbler. You just can&#8217;t beat it. It&#8217;s so rich and simple to make. One of the reasons I love it so much is because it has my favorite biscuit topping. I&#8217;ve been making these biscuits for years and they are so delicious. They go so perfectly on top of these apples. </p>



<p class="has-text-align-center">I&#8217;m telling y&#8217;all; this is a dessert for all year round. When I think of anything cinnamon and apple, I always think of Fall. However, this is a perfect summertime dessert as well. </p>

<h2 class="wp-block-heading">Questions You Might Have:</h2>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading">What type of apples are best for apple cobbler?</h3>



<p>To me, it really doesn&#8217;t matter what type of apple you use for apple cobbler. Always like gala or Fuji apples. That&#8217;s just me. Any variety will work. They are all going to cook down in the cinnamon sugar anyway.</p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading">Do I have to peel my apples?</h3>



<p>I would definitely recommend this. If not, you may get an unpleasant texture of the skin once it all bakes down. Just makes for a smoother, more delicious bite.</p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading">Can I substitute something for the Crisco?</h3>



<p>Yes. I understand that it&#8217;s not for everyone. I would a half stick of very softened butter instead. </p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading">Apple cobbler vs apple crisp?</h3>



<p>This recipe is for an apple cobbler. This is a cinnamon sugar apple base with a flour, biscuit-like topping. An apple crisp recipe is very similar, but the topping is predominantly made with oats.</p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-left">Can you make ahead or freeze this recipe?</h3>



<p class="has-text-align-left">You can make this recipe ahead. I would bake this recipe completely, then freeze it. It can store in the freezer for up to three or so months. Breads and biscuits freeze very well. You may just need to thaw it out and warm it up in the oven again on 325 for about 15-20 minutes.</p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-left">What to serve with apple cobbler?</h3>



<p class="has-text-align-left">Honestly, there is nothing better than eating hot apple cobbler with a giant scoop of vanilla ice cream on top. Extra points if you&#8217;re eating it with <a href="https://turnrowtable.com/old-fashioned-homemade-ice-cream/" data-type="post" data-id="18364">homemade vanilla ice cream</a>. However, it&#8217;s super good solo, but you can also top it with whipped cream or even a caramel sauce.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">

You have to top with vanilla ice cream while it's hot. You cannot beat this classic southern dessert." class="wp-image-18652" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="Savor a southern apple cobbler with a biscuit topping—cinnamon-spiced apples and a buttery crust for a delightful treat." data-jpibfi-post-url="https://turnrowtable.com/simple-skillet-apple-cobbler/" data-jpibfi-post-title="Simple Skillet Apple Cobbler" data-jpibfi-src="https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/apple-cobbler-recipe-683x1024.jpeg" srcset="https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/apple-cobbler-recipe-683x1024.jpeg 683w, https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/apple-cobbler-recipe-200x300.jpeg 200w, https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/apple-cobbler-recipe-768x1152.jpeg 768w, https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/apple-cobbler-recipe-scaled.jpeg 1707w" sizes="(max-width: 683px) 100vw, 683px" /></noscript></figure>
</div>


<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-left">Equipment You&#8217;ll Need</h2>



<p class="has-text-align-left">As for equipment, you&#8217;ll start with a vegetable peeler to peel your apples with. You could leave the rind on, but it&#8217;ll make for a tougher and chewy textured filling. You&#8217;ll then need a skillet to fry your apples and bake the cobbler in. I used a 10-inch cast iron.</p>



<div class="wp-block-group is-nowrap is-layout-flex wp-container-core-group-is-layout-ad2f72ca wp-block-group-is-layout-flex">
<figure class="wp-block-image size-full is-resized"><a href="https://rstyle.me/+_MttwtVktMrL0Pxzza5ppA" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" width="637" height="436" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20637%20436'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="" class="wp-image-18207" style="width:479px;height:auto" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="Savor a southern apple cobbler with a biscuit topping—cinnamon-spiced apples and a buttery crust for a delightful treat." data-jpibfi-post-url="https://turnrowtable.com/simple-skillet-apple-cobbler/" data-jpibfi-post-title="Simple Skillet Apple Cobbler" data-jpibfi-src="https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/10-inch-round-skillet.png" data-lazy-srcset="https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/10-inch-round-skillet.png 637w, https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/10-inch-round-skillet-300x205.png 300w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 637px) 100vw, 637px" data-lazy-src="https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/10-inch-round-skillet.png" /><noscript><img decoding="async" width="637" height="436" src="https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/10-inch-round-skillet.png" alt="" class="wp-image-18207" style="width:479px;height:auto" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="Savor a southern apple cobbler with a biscuit topping—cinnamon-spiced apples and a buttery crust for a delightful treat." data-jpibfi-post-url="https://turnrowtable.com/simple-skillet-apple-cobbler/" data-jpibfi-post-title="Simple Skillet Apple Cobbler" data-jpibfi-src="https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/10-inch-round-skillet.png" srcset="https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/10-inch-round-skillet.png 637w, https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/10-inch-round-skillet-300x205.png 300w" sizes="(max-width: 637px) 100vw, 637px" /></noscript></a></figure>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><a href="https://rstyle.me/+qCE6fiN1U5JjS8hKo3gXcg" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" width="276" height="219" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20276%20219'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="" class="wp-image-32299" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="Savor a southern apple cobbler with a biscuit topping—cinnamon-spiced apples and a buttery crust for a delightful treat." data-jpibfi-post-url="https://turnrowtable.com/simple-skillet-apple-cobbler/" data-jpibfi-post-title="Simple Skillet Apple Cobbler" data-jpibfi-src="https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/10/Screenshot_19-5-2025_93535_creator.shopltk.com_.jpeg" data-lazy-src="https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/10/Screenshot_19-5-2025_93535_creator.shopltk.com_.jpeg" ><noscript><img decoding="async" width="276" height="219" src="https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/10/Screenshot_19-5-2025_93535_creator.shopltk.com_.jpeg" alt="" class="wp-image-32299" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="Savor a southern apple cobbler with a biscuit topping—cinnamon-spiced apples and a buttery crust for a delightful treat." data-jpibfi-post-url="https://turnrowtable.com/simple-skillet-apple-cobbler/" data-jpibfi-post-title="Simple Skillet Apple Cobbler" data-jpibfi-src="https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/10/Screenshot_19-5-2025_93535_creator.shopltk.com_.jpeg" ></noscript></a></figure>
</div>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-left">Ingredients You&#8217;ll Need</h2>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-left">Apples</h3>



<p>You&#8217;ll need 6 to 8 of your apples of choice. I like gala apples, but it&#8217;s up to you. You can also do a mix!</p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-left">Lemon Juice</h3>



<p>This will just help cut down on the tartness of the apples.</p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-left">Butter</h3>



<p>You&#8217;ll need a few tablespoons of butter for your apple filling. </p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-left">Sugars</h3>



<p>You&#8217;ll need a cup of brown sugar for the apple filling. You&#8217;ll also need a half cup of granulated sugar to go in your biscuit dough.</p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-left">Cornstarch</h3>



<p>This will just help thicken up your apple filling. </p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-left">Milk</h3>



<p>You&#8217;ll need a cup of milk to go in your biscuit dough. </p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-left">Flour and Baking Soda</h3>



<p>You&#8217;ll need two cups of flour and a dash of baking soda for your biscuits.</p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-left">Crisco or Shortening</h3>



<p>I used two tablespoons of Crisco. This is just an old tried and true biscuit recipe I&#8217;ve been making for years. If you don&#8217;t want to use the shortening, substitute it for a half stick of softened butter. </p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column18648_249c0b-70"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">How to Make Apple Cobbler</h2>



<ol class="wp-block-list">
<li>Preheat your oven to 350 degrees. Peel and slice your apples and add them to your skillet on medium to high heat with some butter and lemon juice. Sauté them for several minutes then add your cinnamon and nutmeg. Once they have cooked all the way down add in your cornstarch, stir then remove from heat.</li>



<li>In a separate bowl, combine the dry ingredients for the biscuits then add in the Crisco and milk. Work together with your hands until it&#8217;s fully mixed together. Pinch off individual pieces of dough and add over the top of the apples.</li>



<li>Bake at 350 for around 20 minutes or until biscuits are golden brown. Serve with vanilla ice cream and enjoy!</li>
</ol>
</div></div>

<h2 class="wprm-recipe-name wprm-block-text-normal">Apple Cobbler with Biscuit Topping</h2> <div class="wprm-spacer"></div>  <div class="wprm-spacer"></div> <div class="wprm-recipe-summary wprm-block-text-normal"><span style="display: block;">Ok. This apple cobbler with biscuit topping. This is my favorite biscuit recipe on top of a brown sugar, cinnamon fried apple filling. This is so decadent and fluffy. You have to top with vanilla ice cream while it&#039;s hot. You cannot beat this classic southern dessert.</span></div> <div class="wprm-spacer" style="height: 25px;"></div>

<div id="recipe-18660-equipment" class="wprm-recipe-equipment-container wprm-block-text-normal" data-recipe="18660"><h3 class="wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-equipment-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none" style="">Equipment</h3><ul class="wprm-recipe-equipment wprm-recipe-equipment-list"><li class="wprm-recipe-equipment-item" style="list-style-type: Skillet</div></li></ul></div> <div id="recipe-18660-ingredients" class="wprm-recipe-ingredients-container wprm-recipe-18660-ingredients-container wprm-block-text-normal wprm-ingredient-style-regular wprm-recipe-images-before" data-recipe="18660" data-servings="4"><h3 class="wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-ingredients-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none" style="">Ingredients</h3><div class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-group"><h4 class="wprm-recipe-group-name wprm-recipe-ingredient-group-name wprm-block-text-bold">Apple Filling</h4><ul class="wprm-recipe-ingredients"><li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" style="list-style-type: disc;" data-uid="0"><span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">6-8</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">Apples, Peeled and Sliced</span></li><li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" style="list-style-type: disc;" data-uid="4"><span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tbsp</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">Lemon Juice</span></li><li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" style="list-style-type: disc;" data-uid="2"><span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">2</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tbsp</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">Butter</span></li><li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" style="list-style-type: disc;" data-uid="3"><span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">Brown Sugar</span></li><li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" style="list-style-type: disc;" data-uid="5"><span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount"> 1 1/2</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tbsp</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">Cinnamon</span></li><li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" style="list-style-type: disc;" data-uid="6"><span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">dash</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">Nutmeg</span></li><li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" style="list-style-type: disc;" data-uid="7"><span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tbsp</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">Cornstarch</span></li></ul></div><div class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-group"><h4 class="wprm-recipe-group-name wprm-recipe-ingredient-group-name wprm-block-text-bold">Biscuit Topping</h4><ul class="wprm-recipe-ingredients"><li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" style="list-style-type: disc;" data-uid="9"><span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">2</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cups</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">Flour</span></li><li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" style="list-style-type: disc;" data-uid="10"><span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/4</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">Baking Soda</span></li><li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" style="list-style-type: disc;" data-uid="11"><span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/2</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup </span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">Sugar</span></li><li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" style="list-style-type: disc;" data-uid="12"><span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">2</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tbsp</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">Crisco or Shortening</span></li><li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" style="list-style-type: disc;" data-uid="13"><span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">Milk</span></li></ul></div></div> <div id="recipe-18660-instructions" class="wprm-recipe-instructions-container wprm-recipe-18660-instructions-container wprm-block-text-normal" data-recipe="18660"><h3 class="wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-instructions-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none" style="">Instructions</h3><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-group"><ol class="wprm-recipe-instructions"><li id="wprm-recipe-18660-step-0-0" class="wprm-recipe-instruction" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text" style="margin-bottom: 5px;"><span style="display: block;">Preheat your oven to 350 degrees. Peel and slice your apples and add them to your skillet on medium to high heat with some butter and lemon juice. Sauté them for several minutes then add your cinnamon and nutmeg. Once they have cooked all the way down add in your cornstarch, stir then remove from heat. </span></div></li><li id="wprm-recipe-18660-step-0-1" class="wprm-recipe-instruction" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text" style="margin-bottom: 5px;"><span style="display: block;">In a separate bowl, combine the dry ingredients for the biscuits then add in the Crisco and milk. Work together with your hands until it&#39;s fully mixed together. Pinch off individual pieces of dough and add over the top of the apples. </span></div></li><li id="wprm-recipe-18660-step-0-2" class="wprm-recipe-instruction" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text" style="margin-bottom: 5px;"><span style="display: block;">Bake at 350 for around 20 minutes or until biscuits are golden brown. Serve with vanilla ice cream and enjoy!</span></div></li></ol></div></div> <div id="recipe-video"></div>  
</div></div></div>

<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img decoding="async" width="683" height="1024" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20683%201024'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Ok. This apple cobbler with biscuit topping. This is my favorite biscuit recipe on top of a brown sugar, cinnamon fried apple filling. This is so decadent and fluffy. You have to top with vanilla ice cream while it's hot. You cannot beat this classic southern dessert." class="wp-image-18655" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="Savor a southern apple cobbler with a biscuit topping—cinnamon-spiced apples and a buttery crust for a delightful treat." data-jpibfi-post-url="https://turnrowtable.com/simple-skillet-apple-cobbler/" data-jpibfi-post-title="Simple Skillet Apple Cobbler" data-jpibfi-src="https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/apple-cobbler-biscuit-topping-683x1024.jpeg" data-lazy-srcset="https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/apple-cobbler-biscuit-topping-683x1024.jpeg 683w, https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/apple-cobbler-biscuit-topping-200x300.jpeg 200w, https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/apple-cobbler-biscuit-topping-768x1152.jpeg 768w, https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/apple-cobbler-biscuit-topping-1024x1536.jpeg 1024w, https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/apple-cobbler-biscuit-topping-1365x2048.jpeg 1365w, https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/apple-cobbler-biscuit-topping-scaled.jpeg 1707w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 683px) 100vw, 683px" data-lazy-src="https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/apple-cobbler-biscuit-topping-683x1024.jpeg" /><noscript><img decoding="async" width="683" height="1024" src="https://turnrowtable.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/apple-cobbler-biscuit-topping-683x1024.jpeg" alt="Ok. </div>


<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Before you go&#8230;</h2>



<p class="has-text-align-center">Please let me know if you made this easy apple cobbler recipe. What did you think? Did you top it with ice cream? Let me know your thoughts <a href="https://turnrowtable.com/contact-us/" data-type="page" data-id="90">here</a> or in the comments below. Happy cooking!</p>
